    function getCookie(cookie_key) {
        var key, val, res;
        //get all cookie
        var oldCookie = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < oldCookie.length; i++) {

            key = oldCookie[i].substr(0, oldCookie[i].indexOf("="));
            val = oldCookie[i].substr(oldCookie[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
            key = key.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
            //find "user_cookie"
            //alert("key :: "+ key);
            if (key == cookie_key) {
                res = val;
                //alert(res);
            }
        }
        if (res == undefined) {
            return null;
        } else {
            //alert(res);
            try {
                res = JSON.parse(res);
                return res.models;
            }
            catch (err) {
                return null;
            }

        }
    }

    function getCookiePersona() {
        var key, val, res;
        //get all cookie
        var oldCookie = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < oldCookie.length; i++) {

            key = oldCookie[i].substr(0, oldCookie[i].indexOf("="));
            val = oldCookie[i].substr(oldCookie[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
            key = key.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");

            if (key == "CUSTOMER_PERSONA") {
                res = val;

            }
        }
        if (res == undefined) {
            return null;
        } else {

            return res;
        }
    }

  <script>
   function GTMPush(query, value) {
        
		if($.cookie('acceptance') != null)
		{
			if (query == "query") {
				dataLayer.push({ "query": value });
			} else if (query == "model") {
				dataLayer.push({ "model": value });
			} else if (query == "question") {
				dataLayer.push({ "question": value });
			} else if (query == "question category") {
				dataLayer.push({ "question category": value });
			} else if (query == "postal code") {
				dataLayer.push({ "postal code": value });
			} else if (query == "name dealer") {
				dataLayer.push({ "name dealer": value });
			} else if (query == "sales - email") {
				dataLayer.push({ "sales - email": value });
			} else if (query == "service - email") {
				dataLayer.push({ "service - email": value });
			} else if (query == "link-url") {
				dataLayer.push({ "link-url": value });
			} else if (query == "name post") {
				dataLayer.push({ "name post": value });
			} else if (query == "name file") {
				dataLayer.push({ "name file": value });
			} else if (query == "namecolor") {
				dataLayer.push({ "namecolor": value });
			} else if (query == "name line") {
				dataLayer.push({ "name line": value });
			} else if (query == "name engine + transmission") {
				dataLayer.push({ "name engine + transmission": value });
			} else if (query == "name interior") {
				dataLayer.push({ "name interior": value });
			} else if (query == "vpv") {
				dataLayer.push({ "vpv": value });
			} else if (query == "formValidated") {
				dataLayer.push({ "formValidated": value });
			} else if (query == "event") {
				dataLayer.push({ "event": value });
			} else if (query == "searchDealer") {
				dataLayer.push({ "searchDealer": value });
			} else if (query == "selectDealer") {
				dataLayer.push({ "selectDealer": value });
			} else if (query == "formSubmitUrl") {
				dataLayer.push({ "formSubmitUrl": value });
			} else if (query == "carModel1Brochure") {
				dataLayer.push({ "carModel1Brochure": value });
			} else if (query == "carModel1TestDrive") {
				dataLayer.push({ "carModel1TestDrive": value });
			} else if (query == "eventMode") {
				dataLayer.push({ "event": value });
			}
			else if (query == "dimension1") {
				dataLayer.push({ "dimension1": value });
			}
			else if (query == "dimension2") {
				dataLayer.push({ "dimension2": value });
			}
		}

    
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
     //<![CDATA[
    function callSearch(e, searchValue) {
        var searchHeaderText = "Zoeken";
        if (searchValue == searchHeaderText) {
            searchValue = " ";
        }
        var url = "/" + document.getElementById("hdnAlias").value + "/?searchtext=" + searchValue;
        if (e) {
            var charCode = e.charCode || e.keyCode || e.which;
            if (charCode == 13) {

                //------------Google Tracking------------------
                GAPush('searchbar', 'search', searchValue);
                GTMPush('query', searchValue);
                //----------------------------------------------

                window.location = url;
                return false;
            }
        }
        else {
            //------------Google Tracking------------------
            GAPush('searchbar', 'search', searchValue);
            GTMPush('query', searchValue);
            //----------------------------------------------

            window.location = url;
            return false;
        }
    }

    function openLinkForBrochure(category) {
        if (category != "")
            GAPush(category, 'click', "request brochure");

        var url = '';
        var target = 'False';

        if (target.toLowerCase() == 'true') {
            target = "_blank";
        }
        else {
            target = "_self";
        }
        window.open(url, target);
        return false;
    }

    function openLinkForTestDrive(category) {
        if (category != "")
            GAPush(category, 'click', "request testdrive");

        var url = '';
        var target = 'False';

        if (target.toLowerCase() == 'true') {
            target = "_blank";
        }
        else {
            target = "_self";
        }
        window.open(url, target);
        return false;
    }


    //]]>
    </script>

                    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
     //<![CDATA[
    $(document).ready(function () {
        languageToggle();
        

        $($(".top-menu").children("ul").children(".phone").get(0)).prev("li").addClass("align-right");

        

        var usrAgent = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
        var isLumia = usrAgent.indexOf("lumia") > -1;

        if (isLumia) {
            $('.model-menu li').each(function () {
                $(this).find(".sub-menu").prev("a").attr("aria-haspopup", "true");
            });
        }

        //Menu
        $('.model-menu li, #top-nav .nav li').hover(function () {
            try {
                clearTimeout($.data(this, 'timer'));
                $('.sub-menu', this).stop(true, true).slideDown('750', 'easeInOutQuint', function () { });
                /*---------Dynamic Positioning----------------*/
                var subMenuWidth = $('.sub-menu', this).width();
                var submenuleftPos = $('.sub-menu', this).offset().left;

                if ((subMenuWidth + submenuleftPos) > $(window).width()) {
                    var submenuLeftDiff = ($(window).width() - (subMenuWidth + submenuleftPos)) + 10;
                    $('.sub-menu', this).css("left", submenuLeftDiff);
                }
                //--Menu pointer
                $('.sub-menu', this).prev('a').addClass('hover');
            } catch (e) { }
            /*--------------------------------------------*/
        }, function () {
            try {
                $.data(this, 'timer', setTimeout($.proxy(function () {
                    if (!$('.sub-menu', this).hasClass('subMenuBLock')) {
                        if ($(window).width() < 767) {
                            $('.sub-menu', this).stop(true, true).slideUp('750', 'easeInOutQuint', function () { });
                            //$('.sub-menu', this).hide();
                        }
                        else {
                            //$('.sub-menu', this).stop(true, true).fadeOut('10', 'easeInOutCirc', function () { });
                            $('.sub-menu', this).hide();
                        }
                        $('.sub-menu', this).prev('a').removeClass('hover'); //--Menu pointer
                    }
                }, this), 30));
            } catch (e) { }
        });
    });
    $(window).load(function () {
        setNavTop();
    });
    $(window).resize(function () {
        setNavTop();
    });
    function setNavTop() {
        if ($(window).width() >= 768 && $(window).width() <= 991) {
            if ($("#ctl00_mmeHeader_topUlSearch").children("li").css('display') == 'none') {
                $("#top-nav").css("top", "0px");
            }
            else {
                $("#top-nav").css("top", "25px");
            }
        }
    };

    function languageToggle() {
        $("#top-nav .ch-lan a").click(function () {
            setTimeout(function () {
                if (!$("#top-nav .ch-lan").hasClass('active')) {
                    $("#top-nav .ch-lan").removeClass("active");
                }
                else {
                    $("#top-nav .ch-lan").addClass("active");
                }
            }, 1000);
        });
    }
    //]]>
    </script>

        if ($(".MMEModelMaster").length < 0) {
            if ((windowWidth >= 750)) {
                if ($('.swiper-legal').closest('section').nextAll('section').length > 0) {

        var windowWidth = $(window).width();
        if ($(".MMEModelMaster").length < 0) {
            if ((windowWidth >= 750)) {
                if ($('.swiper-legal').closest('section').nextAll('section').length > 0) {

                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  //<![CDATA[
            var call2_action_banner_bottom = "";
            $(window).load(function () {
                call2_action_banner_bottom = $('.call2-action-banner.desktop').css("bottom");

                $(".cta_sticky").hide();
                CTAMobileVisible("winload");
                if ($(window).width() < 768) {
                    $(".mob-model-footer").hide();
                }
                // isOverlap();
            });
            $(window).resize(function () {
                CTAMobileVisible("winresize");
                isOverlap();
            });
            var lastScrollTop = 0;
            $(window).scroll(function (event) {
                var st = $(this).scrollTop();
                if (st > lastScrollTop) {
                    CTAMobileVisible("windownscroll");

                } else {
                    CTAMobileVisible("winupscroll");
                }
                lastScrollTop = st;
                isOverlap();
            });
            //is overlap
            function isOverlap() {
                 
                return;
                 
                try {

                    var CTAoffset_bottom = $('#MMEVideoSlider').offset().top + $('#MMEVideoSlider').outerHeight();
                    var cookieTop = $('.sanoma-optin-bar').offset().top;
                    if (cookieTop < CTAoffset_bottom)
                        UpliftCTA();
                    else
                        $('.call2-action-banner').css("bottom", call2_action_banner_bottom);
                } catch (e) {

                }

            }
            // uplift the CTA buttons if cookie div is present
            function UpliftCTA() {
                var cookieHeight = $('.sanoma-optin-bar').height() + 5 + parseInt(call2_action_banner_bottom, 10);
                console.log(cookieHeight);
                if ($(window).width() >= 768 && $('.sanoma-optin-bar').length > 0) {
                    if ($('.sanoma-optin-bar').css("display") != "none") {
                        $('.call2-action-banner').css("bottom", cookieHeight);
                    }
                    else {
                        $('.call2-action-banner').css("bottom", call2_action_banner_bottom);
                    }
                }
            }
            // find CTA buttons are visible or not in mobile device and add class as visibility needed
            function CTAMobileVisible(callmethods) {
                if ($(window).width() < 768) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        try {
                            if (isiPhone()) {
                                CTAIphone(callmethods);
                            }
                            else {
                                CTAMoveOthers(callmethods);
                            }
                        } catch (e) { };
                    }, 100);
                }
            }
            $(window).bind('orientationchange', function (e) {
                CTAMobileVisible("winorientationchange");
            });
            function CTAMoveOthers(callmethod) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    var CTApartialVisible = $(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(true); // cta button is partial visible
                    var CTAFullVisible = $(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(false); // cta button is full visible
                    var LogoFullVisible = $(".brand").eq(0).visible(true);
                    var FooterFullVisible = $(".mobile-fot-link").visible(false);
                    var topVisible = false;
                    if ($(window).scrollTop() == 0) {
                        topVisible = true;
                    }

                    var bannerPartialVisible = $("#section-1").visible(true);
                    var CTAStickyVisible = $(".cta_sticky").visible(true);
                    if (!CTApartialVisible) {
                        if (!FooterFullVisible) {
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                        }
                        else {
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "");
                        }
                        if ((callmethod == "winload" || callmethod == "winresize") && bannerPartialVisible && topVisible)  // called at window load and at that time banner and logo is visible
                        {
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeIn("fast");
                        }
                        if (callmethod == "windownscroll" && bannerPartialVisible && topVisible) //  called at down scroll and at that time banner and logo is visible
                        {
                            //console.log("down1");
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeIn("fast");
                        }
                        else if (callmethod == "windownscroll" && !bannerPartialVisible) //  called at down scroll and at that time banner is visible
                        {
                            //console.log("down2");
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeOut("fast");
                        }
                        else if (callmethod == "windownscroll" && bannerPartialVisible && LogoFullVisible) //  called at down scroll and at that time banner is visible but not logo
                        {
                            //console.log("down4");
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeIn("fast");
                        }
                        else if (callmethod == "winupscroll" && !bannerPartialVisible) //  called at up scroll and at that time banner is not visible
                        {
                            //console.log("up1");
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeIn("fast");
                        }
                        else if (callmethod == "winupscroll" && bannerPartialVisible && topVisible) //  called at up scroll and at that time banner and logo is visible
                        {
                            //console.log("up2");
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeIn("fast", function () {
                                $(this).show();
                                $(this).find(".call2-action-banner").css({ display: "block" });
                            });
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(".cta_sticky").fadeOut("fast", function () {
                            $(this).css({ display: "none" });
                        });
                    }
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        if ((callmethod == "winload" || callmethod == "winresize") && bannerPartialVisible && topVisible && !$(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(false)) {
                            $(".cta_sticky").show();
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                        }
                    }, 300);
                }, 500);
            }
            function CTAIphone(callmethod) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    var CTApartialVisibleI = $(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(true); // cta button is partial visible
                    var CTAFullVisibleI = $(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(false); // cta button is full visible
                    var LogoFullVisibleI = $(".brand").eq(0).visible(true);
                    var FooterFullVisibleI = $(".mobile-fot-link.stickyFooter").visible(false);
                    var FooterBacktoTopVisibleI = $(".showMenuLeft.menu-btm.fl").visible(true);
                    var topVisibleI = false;
                    if ($(window).scrollTop() == 0) {
                        topVisibleI = true;
                    }
                    var bannerPartialVisibleI = $("#section-1").visible(true);
                    if (FooterBacktoTopVisibleI) {
                        $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "30px");
                    }
                    if (!CTApartialVisibleI) {
                        if (!FooterFullVisibleI) {
                            //  $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                        }
                        else {
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "");
                        }

                        if ((callmethod == "winload" || callmethod == "winresize") && topVisibleI)  // called at window load and at that time banner and logo is visible
                        {
                            $(".cta_sticky").fadeIn("fast");

                        }
                        else if (callmethod == "winupscroll" && topVisibleI) //  called at up scroll and at that time banner and logo is visible
                        {
                            $(".cta_sticky").show();
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                        }
                        else if (callmethod == "windownscroll" && topVisibleI) //  called at up scroll and at that time banner and logo is visible
                        {
                            $(".cta_sticky").show();
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        $(".cta_sticky").fadeOut("fast");
                    }
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        if ((callmethod == "winload" || callmethod == "winorientationchange") && topVisibleI && !$(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(false)) {
                            $(".cta_sticky").show();
                            $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                        }
                        if ((callmethod == "winorientationchange") && topVisibleI && !$(".call2-action-banner.phone.clearfix").eq(0).visible(false)) {
                            $(".cta_sticky").show();
                            if (!$(".mobile-fot-link.stickyFooter").visible(false)) {
                                $(".cta_sticky").css("bottom", "0px");
                            }
                        }
                    }, 400);
                }, 300);
            }

            function iPhoneversion() {
                if (/iP(hone)/.test(navigator.platform)) {
                    // supports iOS 2.0 and later:
                    var v = (navigator.appVersion).match(/OS (\d+)_(\d+)_?(\d+)?/);
                    return [parseInt(v[1], 10), parseInt(v[2], 10), parseInt(v[3] || 0, 10)];
                }
                else {
                    return [0];
                }
            }

            function isiPhone() {
                return (
                    (navigator.platform.indexOf("iPhone") != -1)
                );
            }


            function GetIEVersionFCS() {
                var sAgent = window.navigator.userAgent;
                var Idx = sAgent.indexOf("MSIE");

                // If IE, return version number.
                if (Idx > 0)
                    return parseInt(sAgent.substring(Idx + 5, sAgent.indexOf(".", Idx)));

                    // If IE 11 then look for Updated user agent string.
                else if (!!navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7\./))
                    return 11;

                else
                    return 0; //It is not IE
            }





            //]]>
                 </script>
                 <input id="hdnDatedata" name="ctl00$MainContentHolder$MainBannerDrpZone$columnDisplay$ctl00$controlcolumn$ctl00$WidgetHost$WidgetHost_widget$hdnDatedata" type="hidden"/>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

            function DetectLocationDL() {
                if ($(window).width() < 767) {
                    getLocation("#txtLocationDL");
                    return false;
                }
            }
            function Redirect() {
                var zipcode = $('#txtLocationDL').val();
                if (zipcode) {
                    var url = $("#HdDealerLocatorSitePath").val() + '?zcode=' + zipcode;
                    window.location.assign(url.toLowerCase());
                }
            }

            $(document).ready(function () {
                $("#ctl00_MainContentHolder_AccessoriesDropZone_columnDisplay_ctl00_controlcolumn_ctl00_WidgetHost_WidgetHost_widget_dvDealerLocatorData").djFitText({
                    MaxWidth: 1366,

            function getLocation(elementID) {
                if (navigator.geolocation) {
                    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function (position) {
                        showPosition(position, elementID)
                    }, function (error) {

                    }, { maximumAge: 600000, timeout: 10000 });
                }
                else {
                    //alert("Geolocation is not supported by this browser.");
                }
            }

            function showPosition(position, elementID) {
                var url = "http://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/geocode/json?latlng=" + position.coords.latitude + "," + position.coords.longitude + "&sensor=true";
                $.support.cors = true; //For enabling cross domain support
                $.getJSON(url, function (data) {
                    $.each(data['results'], function (i, val) {
                        $.each(val['address_components'], function (i, val) {
                            if (val['types'] == "postal_code") {
                                if (val['long_name'] != "") {
                                    $(elementID).val(val['long_name']);
                                    if (val['long_name']) {
                                        var url = $("#HdDealerLocatorSitePath").val() + '?zcode=' + val['long_name'] + '&lat=' + position.coords.latitude + '&longt=' + position.coords.longitude;
                                        window.location.assign(url);
                                    }
                                }
                                else {
                                    if (val['types'] == "locality,political") {
                                        if (val['long_name'] != "") {
                                            $(elementID).val(val['long_name']);
                                            if (val['long_name']) {
                                                var url = $("#HdDealerLocatorSitePath").val() + '?zcode=' + val['long_name'] + '&lat=' + position.coords.latitude + '&longt=' + position.coords.longitude;
                                                window.location.assign(url);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            $(elementID).val("unknown");
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    });
                });
                return false;
            }

            // add ajax transport method for cross domain requests when using IE9
            if ('XDomainRequest' in window && window.XDomainRequest !== null) {
                $.ajaxTransport("+*", function (options, originalOptions, jqXHR) {
                    // verify if we need to do a cross domain request
                    // if not return so we don't break same domain requests
                    if (typeof options.crossDomain === 'undefined' || !options.crossDomain) {
                        return;
                    }

                    var xdr;

                    return {
                        send: function (headers, completeCallback) {
                            // Use Microsoft XDR
                            xdr = new XDomainRequest();
                            xdr.open("get", options.url); // NOTE: make sure protocols are the same otherwise this will fail silently
                            xdr.onload = function () {
                                if (this.contentType.match(/\/xml/)) {
                                    var dom = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLDOM");
                                    dom.async = false;
                                    dom.loadXML(this.responseText);
                                    completeCallback(200, "success", [dom]);
                                } else {
                                    completeCallback(200, "success", [this.responseText]);
                                }
                            };

                            xdr.onprogress = function () { };

                            xdr.ontimeout = function () {
                                completeCallback(408, "error", ["The request timed out."]);
                            };

                            xdr.onerror = function () {
                                completeCallback(404, "error", ["The requested resource could not be found."]);
                            };

                            xdr.send();
                        },
                        abort: function () {
                            if (xdr) xdr.abort();
                        }
                    };
                });
            }

            function MaintainMyMitsubishiMargin() {
                var rightSecTotalHeight = $(".my-mitsu-home").height() + $(".my-mitsu-home").parents("li").prev().height();
                var marginDiff = -(rightSecTotalHeight - $(".my-mitsu-home").parents("li").prev().prev().height());

                if (marginDiff > -50 && marginDiff < 100) {
                    marginDiff = marginDiff - 2;
                    $(".my-mitsu-home").css("marginTop", marginDiff);
                } else {
                    setTimeout(function () { MaintainMyMitsubishiMargin() }, 500);
                }
            }

            function GATrack(media) {
                var eventLabel = "";
                //alert(media);
                switch (media) {
                    case "facebook":
                        eventLabel = "fb";
                        break;
                    case "twitter":
                        eventLabel = "twitter";
                        break;
                    case "instagram":
                        eventLabel = "instagram";
                        break;
                    case "youtube":
                        eventLabel = "youtube";
                        break;
                    case "google":
                        eventLabel = "google+";
                        break;
                }
                GAPush('social media', 'social room', eventLabel);
            }

    // Array Sorting
    var delarArry = [];
    var sortType = "";
    delarArry.sort(function (a, b) {
        var sortStatus = 0;

        if (a < b) {
            sortStatus = -1;
        } else if (a > b) {
            sortStatus = 1;
        }

        return sortStatus;
    });

    function sortByDistanceOrder(a, b) {
        var sortStatus = 0;

        if (parseFloat(a.distance) < parseFloat(b.distance)) {
            sortStatus = -1;
        } else if (parseFloat(a.distance) > parseFloat(b.distance)) {
            sortStatus = 1;
        }
        return sortStatus;
    }

    var firstddlOpt = null;
    var alltddlOpt = null;
    var isFirstTime = true;

    function populateDealerOnLatLon(lat, lon) {
        //console.log('fire call back');
        //console.log(lat);
        //console.dir(allDealerVal);
        debugger;
        delarArry = []
        var dropdown = $("#frmRequestToTestDrive").find("#Dealer");

        if (isFirstTime) {
            var oppts = $(dropdown).find('option');
            if (oppts != null && oppts.length > 0) {
                firstddlOpt = oppts[0];
                alltddlOpt = oppts;
            }

            isFirstTime = false;
        }

        if (sessionStorage != null && allDealerVal == null) {
            console.log('from FilteredDelears session');
            var allDealer = sessionStorage.getItem('FilteredDelears');
            allDealerVal = JSON.parse(allDealer);
        }

        if (allDealerVal != null && allDealerVal.length > 0) {
            if (lat != null && lon != null) {
                $.each(allDealerVal, function (indx, dealer) {
                      
                    if (dealer.Id == '19999') {
                        return;
                    }
                    

                    var distance = getDistanceFromLatLonInKm(lat, lon, dealer.Lat, dealer.Long);
                    dealer.distance = parseInt(distance);
                    dealer.lable = dealer.City + " (" + dealer.distance + " km) " + dealer.ZipCodePostalCode + " " + dealer.DealerName;
                    delarArry.push(dealer);
                    // delarArry.push({ 'distance': parseInt(distance), 'label': dealer.Name, 'value': dealer.WorkingHoursID, 'city': dealer.City, 'zip': dealer.ZipCodePostalCode, 'dealerName': dealer.DealerName });
                });

                delarArry = delarArry.sort(sortByDistanceOrder);

                //console.log('lat lon filter');
                var data = delarArry.slice(0, 3);
                //$(data).empty();
                $(dropdown).empty();

                if (firstddlOpt != null && firstddlOpt != "")
                    $(dropdown).append(firstddlOpt);
                FillDealerRTD2(data);
                /*  $(data).each(function () {
                     var lable = this.city + " (" + this.distance + " km) " + this.zip + " " + this.dealerName;
                     $("<option />", {
                         val: this.value,
                         text: lable
                     }).appendTo(dropdown);
                 });*/

                $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                $(dropdown).find('option:eq(1)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                $(dropdown).customSelect();
            }
            else {
                //console.log('no lat lon filter');
                $(dropdown).empty();
                if (alltddlOpt != null) {
                    $(dropdown).append(alltddlOpt);
                    $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                    $(dropdown).find('option:eq(0)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                    $(dropdown).customSelect();
                }
                else {
                    $.each(allDealerVal, function (indx, dealer) {
                        var distance = 0.0;
                        delarArry.push({ 'distance': distance, 'label': dealer.Name, 'value': dealer.WorkingHoursID });
                    });
                    //console.dir(delarArry);
                    $(dropdown).empty();
                    $(delarArry).each(function () {
                        $("<option />", {
                            val: this.value,
                            text: this.label
                        }).appendTo(dropdown);
                    });
                }
                $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                $(dropdown).find('option:eq(0)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                $(dropdown).customSelect();
            }
        }
        else {
            $(dropdown).empty();
            if (alltddlOpt != null && $(dropdown).find('option').length < 4) {
                $(dropdown).append(alltddlOpt);
                $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                $(dropdown).find('option:eq(0)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                $(dropdown).customSelect();
            }
        }

    }

    function getDistanceFromLatLonInKm(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
        var R = 6371; // Radius of the earth in km
        var dLat = deg2rad(lat2 - lat1);  // deg2rad below
        var dLon = deg2rad(lon2 - lon1);
        var a =
          Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
          Math.cos(deg2rad(lat1)) * Math.cos(deg2rad(lat2)) *
          Math.sin(dLon / 2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2)
        ;
        var c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
        var d = R * c; // Distance in km
        return d;
    }

    function deg2rad(deg) {
        return deg * (Math.PI / 180)
    }

    function getNationalHolidays() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            dataType: "json",
            url: "/layouts/Handlers/ReadHolidayList.ashx",
            success: function (data, status) {
                var dateArray = "";
                if (data != "" && data.indexOf(',') != -1) {
                    dateArray = data.split(',');
                }
                //else {
                //    arrDisabledDates = "dates";
                //}
                if (dateArray.length > 0) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < dateArray.length; i++) {
                        arrDisabledDates[new Date(dateArray[i])] = new Date(dateArray[i]);
                    }
                }
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {
                //alert(status);
            }
        });
    }


    function FillModelRTD(objArr) {

        var modelNameRB = $('[id$="hdnModelMarketingName"]').val(); // model page has a hidden control whose name is hdnModelName, this hepls to find the id whose lastpart is hdnModelName. the generated id something like 'ctl00_MainContentHolder_CarConfiguratorDropZone_columnDisplay_ctl00_controlcolumn_ctl00_WidgetHost_WidgetHost_widget_hdnModelName'
        var selectModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel1");
        var selectModel2 = $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel2");
        //alert("FillModelRTD called: " + modelNameRB);

        if ($('[id$="hdnModelMarketingName"]').val() != undefined) {
            
        }
        else {
            if ($('[id$="hdnmodelPreselect"]').val() != "") {
                modelNameRB = $('[id$="hdnmodelPreselect"]').val().trim();
            }
            else {
                modelNameRB = '';
            }
        }


        if ($("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel1 option").size() > 1) {
            if (modelNameRB != undefined && $.trim(modelNameRB) != "") {
                selectModel1.find("option:selected").removeAttr('selected');
                selectModel1.find("option[value='" + modelNameRB + "']").attr('selected', 'selected');
                selectModel1.next().children().text(modelNameRB);
            }
            return;
        }
        if (objArr) {
            $(objArr).each(function (index, item) {
                if (item.IsNonPCCModel == false && item.ShowInTestDriveForm == true) {

                    if (item.Name.replace(/\-{1,}/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase() == modelNameRB.replace(/\-{1,}/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase()) {
                        //alert("RD Model Name: " + modelNameRB.replace(/\-{1,}/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase());
                        selectModel1.find("option:selected").removeAttr('selected');
                        selectModel1.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name).attr('selected', 'selected'));
                        selectModel1.next().children().text(item.Name);
                    }
                    else {
                        selectModel1.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                    }

                }
                else {

                    if (item.RTDPosition1 == true) {
                        selectModel1.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                    }
                }

                if (item.IsNonPCCModel == false && item.ShowInTestDriveForm == true) {
                    selectModel2.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                }
                else {
                    if (item.RTDPosition2 == true) {
                        selectModel2.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        hide2ndCarmodelonLoad();// cal this function after loading the models
    }

    function loadModelRTD(hasval) {
        //alert("loadModelRTD called");

                dataType: "json",
                success: function (data) {

                    FillModelRTD(data.d);
                }
            });
        }

    }

    var allDealerVal = null;
    function loadPreferredDelearRTD(hasval) {

                type: "POST",
                url: "/services/WebService.asmx/GetFilteredDelears",

                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (data) {
                    console.log('loadPreferredDelearRTD fire');
                    arrDealer = data.d;
                    if (sessionStorage != null)
                        sessionStorage.setItem('FilteredDelears', JSON.stringify(arrDealer));
                    allDealerVal = data.d;
                    FillDealerRTD(data.d);
                }

            });

        }
    }


    function GetMOISettingsValueRTD(Key) {

        var jsonData = JSON.parse(moiSettings);
        var resultValue = 0;
        if (jsonData.length > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < jsonData.length; i++) {
                if (jsonData[i]["Text"] == Key) {
                    resultValue = parseInt(jsonData[i]["Value"]);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return resultValue;
    }

    function SetMOIScoreRTDCookie(Score, selectedModel) {
        var CarModelID = selectedModel;
        var initialConfiguration = 1;
        //var Score = 1;
        var cookie_key = "MOI_SCORE";
        domainValue = window.location.host;

        setCarConfiguratorRTDCookie(cookie_key, domainValue, initialConfiguration, CarModelID, Score);
        //ev.stopPropagation();
    }

    function getCookieRTD(cookie_key) {
        var key, val, res;
        //get all cookie
        var oldCookie = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < oldCookie.length; i++) {

            key = oldCookie[i].substr(0, oldCookie[i].indexOf("="));
            val = oldCookie[i].substr(oldCookie[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
            key = key.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
            //find "user_cookie"
            //alert("key :: "+ key);
            if (key == cookie_key) {
                res = val;
                //alert(res);
            }
        }
        if (res == undefined) {
            return null;
        } else {
            //alert(res);
            try {
                res = JSON.parse(res);

                return res.models;
            }
            catch (err) {
                return null;
            }

        }
    }

    function setCarConfiguratorRTDCookie(cookie_key, domainValue, InitialValue, CarModelID, Score) {
        var arr = new Array();
        var obj = new Object();
        var flag = false;

        var HighestValue = 0;
        var HighestvalueModel;

        //get old cookie data
        var temp = getCookieRTD(cookie_key);

        if (temp != null) {
            //concat new and old cookie data
            for (var i = 0; i < temp.length; i++) {
                var ob = new Object();

                ob.ModelID = temp[i].ModelID;
                if (temp[i].ModelID == CarModelID) {
                    ob.Hits = temp[i].Hits + 1;
                }
                else {
                    ob.Hits = temp[i].Hits;
                }
                ob.LastScore = Score;
                if (temp[i].Hits + InitialValue == 2) {
                    if (temp[i].ModelID == CarModelID) {
                        ob.Score = Score + temp[i].Score + temp[i].LastScore;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRTD(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                        flag = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        ob.Score = temp[i].Score;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRTD(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                    }
                }
                else if (temp[i].Hits + InitialValue > 2) {
                    if (temp[i].ModelID == CarModelID) {

                        ob.Score = Score + temp[i].Score;
                        //alert("in model 2:: " + ob.Score + "   " + temp[i].Score + "   " + Score);
                        flag = true;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRTD(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        ob.Score = temp[i].Score;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRTD(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                    }
                }
                //alert("in model else:: " + ob.ModelID + "   " + ob.LastScore + "   " + ob.Score + "   " + ob.Hits);
                arr.push(ob);
            }
        }

        if (flag == false) {
            obj.ModelID = CarModelID;
            obj.Hits = InitialValue;
            obj.LastScore = Score;
            obj.Score = 0;
            if (obj.Score >= HighestValue) {
                HighestvalueModel = obj.ModelID;
                SETMOICookieRTD(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
            }
            arr.push(obj);
        }

        var objWarp = new Object();
        objWarp.models = arr;
        var val = JSON.stringify(objWarp);
        //alert("val:: "+val);
        //set cookie date expired
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();

        //create cookie
        document.cookie = cookie_key + "=" + val + ";domain=." + domainValue + ";path=/";

    }

    function SETMOICookieRTD(HighestvalueModel, domainValue) {
        //alert("Moi Cookie");
        var arr = new Array();
        var obj = new Object();
        obj.ModelID = HighestvalueModel;
        arr.push(obj);
        var objWarp = new Object();
        objWarp.models = arr;
        var val = JSON.stringify(objWarp);
        //alert("Value ::"+val);
        //set cookie date expired
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
        //create cookie
        document.cookie = "MOI_Temp" + "=" + val + expires + ";domain=." + domainValue + ";path=/";
        //alert(getCookie("MOI")[0].ModelID);
    }

            catch (e) {
                console.error(e);
            }
        }
        //----------------------------------------------

        //Set Targeted Content Cookie
        try {
            var ScoreValue = GetMOISettingsValueRTD("RequestTestDrive");
            SetMOIScoreRTDCookie(ScoreValue, TestDriveCarModel1);
        }
        catch (err) {

        }

        //Google Tracking on form submit for selected model
        GoogleTrackingModelSelectionRTD();
        if ('NL' == 'NL') {
            if ('true' == 'true') {
                SalesForceRTD();
            }

        }

        
        $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#dvFormSubmitData").fadeOut("slow");
        $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("ektdesignns_choices").fadeOut("slow");
        var message = "<div id=\"dvMessage\" class=\"pro-more-cont form-msg form-display-msg\">" + document.getElementById("RTDlblMessage").innerHTML + "</div>";
        $(message).insertAfter($("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#dvFormSubmitData"));

        // Change in Position
        $(".fancybox-wrap").css("top", $(window).scrollTop() + 20);
        

        //PT | Insert pixelcode to CTA buttons jira -1494
        if ('NL' == 'PT') {
            var modelName = "";
            var hdnSelectedModelName = "hdnSelectedModelName";
            modelName = $('#' + hdnSelectedModelName).val();
            console.log('carModel selecetd in PT pixel code is ' + modelName);
            firePTpixelCodeRTD(modelName);
        }

    }
    //For PT only jira -1494
    function firePTpixelCodeRTD(modelName) {
        try {

            console.log('firePTpixelCode | for modelName:' + modelName);
            if (modelName == null || modelName == "")
                return;
            modelName = modelName.toLowerCase();

            if (modelName.indexOf("asx") > -1) {

                console.log('firePTpixelCode | for asx:');

                fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                    content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                    content_category: 'ASX'
                });
            }
            else
                if (modelName.indexOf("space star") > -1) {

                    console.log('firePTpixelCode | for space star');

                    fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                        content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                        content_category: 'SpaceStar'
                    });
                }
                else
                    if (modelName.indexOf("outlander di") > -1) {

                        console.log('firePTpixelCode | for outlander di');

                        fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                            content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                            content_category: 'Outlander-Did'
                        });
                    }
                    else
                        if (modelName.indexOf("outlander") > -1 && modelName.indexOf("phev") > -1) {

                            console.log('firePTpixelCode | for outlander phev');

                            fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                                content_category: 'Outlander-Phev'
                            });
                        }
                        else
                            if (modelName.indexOf("i-miev") > -1) {

                                console.log('firePTpixelCode | for i-miev');

                                fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                    content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                                    content_category: 'iMiEV'
                                });
                            }
                            else
                                if (modelName.indexOf("l200") > -1) {

                                    console.log('firePTpixelCode | for l200');

                                    fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                        content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                                        content_category: 'L200'
                                    });
                                }
                                else
                                    if (modelName.indexOf("pajero") > -1) {

                                        console.log('firePTpixelCode | for pajero');

                                        fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                            content_name: 'MarcarTesteDrive',
                                            content_category: 'Pajero'
                                        });
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        console.log('No! pixel code has been fire in MarcarTesteDrive firePTpixelCode | for modelName:' + modelName);
                                    }

        }
        catch (e) {
            console.log('Error! occour in firePTpixelCode | for modelName:' + modelName);
            console.error(e);
        }
    }

    function FillPromoScriptRTD(objPromo) {

        if (objPromo != null) {
            var ifrm = document.getElementById('RTDPromoFrame');
            ifrm = (ifrm.contentWindow) ? ifrm.contentWindow : (ifrm.contentDocument.document) ? ifrm.contentDocument.document : ifrm.contentDocument;
            ifrm.document.open();
            ifrm.document.write(objPromo);
            ifrm.document.close();
        }

    }

    function ExecutePromotionalScriptRTD(hasVal) {

        if (hasVal) {
            FillPromoScriptRTD(objPromoScriptRTD)
        }
        else {
            var actualUrl = window.location.pathname;
            var HashUrl = window.location.hash;
            var hostUrl = document.location.protocol + "//" + document.location.hostname;
            var pageUrl;
            if (HashUrl != "") {
                pageUrl = actualUrl + HashUrl;
            }
            else { pageUrl = actualUrl; }
            promourl = pageUrl;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "json",
                data: { 'CallingUrl': pageUrl },
                url: hostUrl + "/layouts/Handlers/GetPromotionalScriptDetails.ashx",
                success: function (data, status) {
                    objPromoScriptRTD = data;
                    FillPromoScriptRTD(data);
                },
                error: function (request, status, error) {
                    //alert(status);
                }
            });
        }



    }


    //Function for disable 2nd car model on selection of the 1st car model
    function hide2ndCarmodel() {

        var dropCarModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel1");
        var dropCarModel2 = $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel2");
        if (dropCarModel1.length == 0 || dropCarModel2.length == 0) {
            return;
        }

        $(dropCarModel1).change(function () {
            var parentvalue = $(dropCarModel1).find("option:selected").text();
            $(dropCarModel2).each(function () {
                $(dropCarModel2).find("option").removeAttr("disabled");
            });
            var select2ndCarText = $(dropCarModel2).find("option")[0].text;
            $(dropCarModel2).find("option[value='" + parentvalue + "']").attr("disabled", "disabled");
            $(dropCarModel2).next("span").children().text(select2ndCarText);

        });
    }

    //Function for disable 2nd car model on Model Page load
    function hide2ndCarmodelonLoad() {
        var dropCarModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel1");
        var dropCarModel2 = $("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel2");
        if (dropCarModel1.length == 0 || dropCarModel2.length == 0) {
            return;
        }
        //var parentvalue = $('[id$="hdnModelMarketingName"]').val();
        var parentvalue = dropCarModel1.next().children().text();

        $(dropCarModel2).each(function () {
            $(dropCarModel2).find("option").removeAttr("disabled");
        });
        var select2ndCarText = $(dropCarModel2).find("option")[0].text;
        $(dropCarModel2).find("option[value='" + parentvalue + "']").attr("disabled", "disabled");
        $(dropCarModel2).next("span").children().text(select2ndCarText);
		
		$("#FrmRequestToTestDrive").find("#CarModel1").removeAttr("disabled");
    }

            //------------Google Tracking------------------        
            GTMPush('formValidated', 'true');
            GAPush('form', 'model selection testdrive request', selectedModel);
            //GAPush('form', 'Event Action', 'Test Drive');
            //----------------------------------------------
        }
    }

    /* google lat lon for dealer selection */
    // Array Sorting
    var delarArry = [];
    var sortType = "";
    delarArry.sort(function (a, b) {
        var sortStatus = 0;

        if (a < b) {
            sortStatus = -1;
        } else if (a > b) {
            sortStatus = 1;
        }

        return sortStatus;
    });

    function sortByDistanceOrder(a, b) {
        var sortStatus = 0;

        if (parseFloat(a.distance) < parseFloat(b.distance)) {
            sortStatus = -1;
        } else if (parseFloat(a.distance) > parseFloat(b.distance)) {
            sortStatus = 1;
        }
        return sortStatus;
    }

    var firstddlOpt = null;
    var alltddlOpt = null;
    var isFirstTime = true;

    function populateDealerOnLatLonBrocheur(lat, lon) {
        //console.log('fire call back');
        // console.log(lat);
        //console.dir(allDealerValBrocheur);
        debugger;
        delarArry = []
        var dropdown = $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer");

        if (isFirstTime) {
            var oppts = $(dropdown).find('option');
            if (oppts != null && oppts.length > 0) {
                firstddlOpt = oppts[0];
                alltddlOpt = oppts;
            }

            isFirstTime = false;
        }

        if (sessionStorage != null && allDealerValBrocheur == null) {
            console.log('from FilteredDelears session');
            var allDealer = sessionStorage.getItem('FilteredDelears');
            allDealerValBrocheur = JSON.parse(allDealer);
        }

        if (allDealerValBrocheur != null && allDealerValBrocheur.length > 0) {
            if (lat != null && lon != null) {
                $.each(allDealerValBrocheur, function (indx, dealer) {
                    
                    if (dealer.Id == '19999') {
                        return;
                    }
                    

                    var distance = getDistanceFromLatLonInKm(lat, lon, dealer.Lat, dealer.Long);
                    dealer.distance = parseInt(distance);
                    dealer.lable = dealer.City + " (" + dealer.distance + " km) " + dealer.ZipCodePostalCode + " " + dealer.DealerName;
                    delarArry.push(dealer);
                    // delarArry.push({ 'distance': parseInt(distance), 'label': dealer.Name, 'value': dealer.WorkingHoursID, 'city': dealer.City, 'zip': dealer.ZipCodePostalCode, 'dealerName': dealer.DealerName });
                });

                delarArry = delarArry.sort(sortByDistanceOrder);

                //console.log('lat lon filter');
                var data = delarArry.slice(0, 3);
                // console.dir(data);
                //$(data).empty();
                $(dropdown).empty();
                if (firstddlOpt != null && firstddlOpt != "")
                    $(dropdown).append(firstddlOpt);
                FillDealerRB2(data);
                /* $(data).each(function () {
                     var lable = this.city + " (" + this.distance + " km) " + this.zip + " " + this.dealerName;
                     $("<option />", {
                         val: this.value,
                         text: lable
                     }).appendTo(dropdown);
                 });*/

                $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                $(dropdown).find('option:eq(1)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                $(dropdown).customSelect();
            }
            else {
                // console.log('no lat lon filter');
                $(dropdown).empty();
                if (alltddlOpt != null) {
                    $(dropdown).append(alltddlOpt);
                    $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                    $(dropdown).find('option:eq(0)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                    $(dropdown).customSelect();
                }
                else {
                    $.each(allDealerValBrocheur, function (indx, dealer) {
                        var distance = 0.0;
                        delarArry.push({ 'distance': distance, 'label': dealer.Name, 'value': dealer.WorkingHoursID });
                    });
                    $(delarArry).each(function () {
                        $("<option />", {
                            val: this.value,
                            text: this.label
                        }).appendTo(dropdown);
                    });
                }
                $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                $(dropdown).find('option:eq(0)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                $(dropdown).customSelect();
            }
        }
        else {
            $(dropdown).empty();
            if (alltddlOpt != null && $(dropdown).find('option').length < 4) {
                $(dropdown).append(alltddlOpt);
                $(dropdown).find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                $(dropdown).find('option:eq(0)').attr('selected', 'selected');
                $(dropdown).customSelect();
            }
        }

    }

    function getDistanceFromLatLonInKm(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
        var R = 6371; // Radius of the earth in km
        var dLat = deg2rad(lat2 - lat1);  // deg2rad below
        var dLon = deg2rad(lon2 - lon1);
        var a =
          Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
          Math.cos(deg2rad(lat1)) * Math.cos(deg2rad(lat2)) *
          Math.sin(dLon / 2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2)
        ;
        var c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
        var d = R * c; // Distance in km
        return d;
    }

    function deg2rad(deg) {
        return deg * (Math.PI / 180)
    }


    function GetAddressInfo() {
        setTimeout(function () {
            try {
                var Street = $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Street");
                var HouseNumber = $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#HouseNumber");
                if (($(Street).val() == "" || $(Street).val() == $(Street).attr('placeholder')) && ($(HouseNumber).val() == "" || $(HouseNumber).val() == $(HouseNumber).attr('placeholder'))) {
                    FillDealerRB(arrDealer);
                    $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val('');
                    $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").val('');
                    if (getInternetExplorerVersion() == "9") {
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").attr('placeholder'));
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").val($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").attr('placeholder'));
                    }
                    streetNames = [];
                    $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").autocomplete({
                        source: streetNames,
                        minLength: 0,
                        appendTo: "#divRTBAutocomplete"
                    }).bind('focus', function () {
                        $(this).autocomplete("search");
                    });
                }
                else {
                    CallDEAPI();
                }
            } catch (e) {
            }
        }, 1000);
    }

    //Dealer Auto Populate Function
    function PopulateDealer(lat, long) {
        if (lat != "" && long != "") {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/services/WebService.asmx/GetDealerByLatLong",
                data: "{'lattitude':'" + lat + "','longitude':'" + long + "'}",
                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (data) {
                    $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer").find(":selected").removeAttr('selected');
                    if (data.d != "") {
                        var count = 0;
                        var options;
                        var option_text = '';
                        var first_match = 0;
                        var arrDealerNearest = data.d.split(',');

                        for (i = 0; i < arrDealerNearest.length; i++) {
                            option = $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option[value='" + arrDealerNearest[i] + "']");
                            if (option.attr('value') != undefined) {
                                first_match = option.attr('value');
                                break;
                            }
                        }

                        for (i = 0; i < arrDealerNearest.length; i++) {
                            option = $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option[value='" + arrDealerNearest[i] + "']");
                            if (option.attr('value') != undefined) {
                                count++;
                                option_text += "<option demail='" + option.attr('demail') + "' dname='" + option.attr('dname') + "' value='" + option.attr('value') + "'>" + option.text() + "</option>";
                                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option[value='" + arrDealerNearest[i] + "']").remove();
                            }
                            if (count == 5)
                                break;
                        }
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer").children('option:not(:first)').remove();
                        $(option_text).insertAfter($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option").eq(0));
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option[value='" + first_match + "']").attr("selected", "selected");
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer").nextAll().find("span.customSelectInner:first").text($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer").find(":selected").text());
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option:first").attr("selected", "selected");
                        $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer").nextAll().find("span.customSelectInner:first").text($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Dealer option:first").text());
                    }
                },
                error: function (e) {
                    return;

                }
            });
        }
        if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Trident") != -1) {
            if (getInternetExplorerVersion() == "11") {
                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#CompanyName").focus();
                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#CompanyName").blur();
            }
        }
    }

    function CallDEAPI() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/layouts/Handlers/GoogleMapApiRTB.ashx",
            dataType: "xml",
            data: { 'Street': $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Street").val(), 'HouseNumber': $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#HouseNumber").val(), 'StreetPlaceholder': $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Street").attr('placeholder'), 'HouseNumberPlaceholder': $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#HouseNumber").attr('placeholder') },
            success: function (msg) {
                if ($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Street").val() != '' || $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#HouseNumber").val() != '') {
                    try {
                        xml = msg;
                        PostalCode = '';
                        $(msg).find('result:first address_component').each(function () {
                            if ($(this).find('type').text() == 'postal_code') {
                                PostalCode = $(this).find('long_name').text();
                            }
                        });
                        $(msg).find('result:first location').each(function () {
                            lati_longi = $(this).find('lat').text() + ',' + $(this).find('lng').text();
                        });

                        //Dealer Auto Populate Function Call
                        if (lati_longi.trim() != "," && $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val() != "" && $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val() != $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").attr('placeholder')) {
                            FillDealerRB(arrDealer);
                            PopulateDealer(lati_longi.split(',')[0], lati_longi.split(',')[1]);
                        }
                        else {
                            FillDealerRB(arrDealer);
                        }
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            if ($('body').find("#divRTBAutocomplete ul.ui-autocomplete").length > 0) {
                                $('body').find("#divRTBAutocomplete ul.ui-autocomplete").addClass('ui-id-1');
                            }
                        }, 200);

                        streetNames = [];
                        if ($(msg).find('result formatted_address').length > 0) {
                            $(msg).find('result formatted_address').each(function () {
                                var temp = $(this).text();
                                $(function () {
                                    if (jQuery.inArray(temp, streetNames) == -1) {
                                        streetNames.push(temp);
                                    }
                                    $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").autocomplete({
                                        source: streetNames,
                                        minLength: 0,
                                        appendTo: "#divRTBAutocomplete"
                                    }).bind('focus', function () {
                                        $(this).autocomplete("search");
                                    });
                                });
                            });
                        }
                        if (PostalCode != '') {
                            //$("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").val('');
                            if (getInternetExplorerVersion() == "9") {
                                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val('');
                            }
                            $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val(PostalCode);
                            if ($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").hasClass('error-msg-input')) {
                                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").removeClass('error-msg-input');
                                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").closest('div').find('.error-msg-txtx').text('');
                            }
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val('');
                            $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").val('');
                            if (getInternetExplorerVersion() == "9") {
                                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").val($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").attr('placeholder'));
                                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").val($("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").attr('placeholder'));
                            }
                            //$("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").focus();
                            //$("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#Zip").blur(); 
                            streetNames = [];
                            $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#City").autocomplete({
                                source: streetNames,
                                minLength: 0,
                                appendTo: "#divRTBAutocomplete"
                            }).bind('focus', function () {
                                $(this).autocomplete("search");
                            });
                        }

                    } catch (e) {
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        if (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Trident") != -1) {

            if (getInternetExplorerVersion() == "11") {
                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#CompanyName").focus();
                $("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("#CompanyName").blur();
                //var nonMandateRTBFound1 = false;               
                //$("#frmRequestToBrochure").find("input[type=text]").each(function ()
                //{
                //    var mandateattr = $(this).attr('ektdesignns_validation');                    
                //    if (typeof mandateattr !== typeof undefined && mandateattr !== false && !nonMandateRTBFound1)
                //    {
                //        nonMandateRTBFound1 = true;
                //        $(this).focus();
                //        $(this).blur();
                //    }                   

                //});            
            }
        }
    }

    function FillModelRB(objArr) {

        var modelNameRB = $('[id$="hdnModelMarketingName"]').val(); // model page has a hidden control whose name is hdnModelName, this hepls to find the id whose lastpart is hdnModelName. the generated id something like 'ctl00_MainContentHolder_CarConfiguratorDropZone_columnDisplay_ctl00_controlcolumn_ctl00_WidgetHost_WidgetHost_widget_hdnModelName'
        var selectModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1");
        var selectModel2 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel2");

        if ($('[id$="hdnModelMarketingName"]').val() != undefined) {
            
        }
        else {
            if ($('[id$="hdnmodelPreselect"]').val() != "") {
                modelNameRB = $('[id$="hdnmodelPreselect"]').val().trim();
            }
            else {
                modelNameRB = '';
            }
        }
        if ($("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1 option").size() > 1) {
            if (modelNameRB != undefined && $.trim(modelNameRB) != "") {
                selectModel1.find("option:selected").removeAttr('selected');
                selectModel1.find("option[value='" + modelNameRB + "']").attr('selected', 'selected');
                selectModel1.next().children().text(modelNameRB);
            }

            return;
        }
        if (objArr) {
            $(objArr).each(function (index, item) {
                if (item.IsNonPCCModel == false && item.ShowInRequestABrochureForm == true) {

                    if (item.Name.replace(/\-{1,}/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase() == modelNameRB.replace(/\-{1,}/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase()) {
                        //alert("RB Model Name: " + modelNameRB.replace(/\-{1,}/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase());
                        selectModel1.find("option:selected").removeAttr('selected');
                        selectModel1.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name).attr('selected', 'selected'));
                        selectModel1.next().children().text(item.Name);
                    }
                    else {
                        selectModel1.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                    }

                }
                else {

                    if (item.RTBPosition1 == true) {
                        selectModel1.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                    }
                }

                if (item.IsNonPCCModel == false && item.ShowInRequestABrochureForm == true) {
                    selectModel2.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                }
                else {
                    if (item.RTBPosition2 == true) {
                        selectModel2.append($("<option>").val(item.Name).text(item.Name));
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        hide2ndCarmodelonLoad();// cal this function after loading the models
    }

    }

    function loadModelRB(hasval) {

        if (hasval) {

                data: "",

                dataType: "json",
