                    FillModelRB(data.d);
                }
            });
        }

    }
    var allDealerValBrocheur = null;
    function loadPreferredDelearRB(hasval) {

        if (hasval) {
            FillDealerRB(arrDealer);
        }
        else {

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/services/WebService.asmx/GetFilteredDelears",
                data: "{ 'strFilterDetails':'" + '1' + "'}",
                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (data) {
                    console.log('loadPreferredDelearRB fire');
                    arrDealer = data.d;
                    if (sessionStorage != null)
                        sessionStorage.setItem('FilteredDelears', JSON.stringify(arrDealer));
                    allDealerValBrocheur = data.d;
                    FillDealerRB(data.d);
                }

            });

        }
    }


    function GetMOISettingsValueRB(Key) {

        var jsonData = JSON.parse(moiSettings);
        var resultValue = 0;
        if (jsonData.length > 0) {
            for (var i = 0; i < jsonData.length; i++) {
                if (jsonData[i]["Text"] == Key) {
                    resultValue = parseInt(jsonData[i]["Value"]);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return resultValue;
    }

    function SetMOIScoreRBCookie(Score, selectedModel) {
        var CarModelID = selectedModel;
        var initialConfiguration = 1;
        //var Score = 1;
        var cookie_key = "MOI_SCORE";
        domainValue = window.location.host;

        setCarConfiguratorRBCookie(cookie_key, domainValue, initialConfiguration, CarModelID, Score);
        //ev.stopPropagation();
    }

    function getCookieRB(cookie_key) {
        var key, val, res;
        //get all cookie
        var oldCookie = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < oldCookie.length; i++) {

            key = oldCookie[i].substr(0, oldCookie[i].indexOf("="));
            val = oldCookie[i].substr(oldCookie[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
            key = key.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
            //find "user_cookie"
            //alert("key :: "+ key);
            if (key == cookie_key) {
                res = val;
                //alert(res);
            }
        }
        if (res == undefined) {
            return null;
        } else {
            //alert(res);
            try {
                res = JSON.parse(res);

                return res.models;
            }
            catch (err) {
                return null;
            }

        }
    }

    function setCarConfiguratorRBCookie(cookie_key, domainValue, InitialValue, CarModelID, Score) {
        var arr = new Array();
        var obj = new Object();
        var flag = false;

        var HighestValue = 0;
        var HighestvalueModel;

        //get old cookie data
        var temp = getCookieRB(cookie_key);

        if (temp != null) {
            //concat new and old cookie data
            for (var i = 0; i < temp.length; i++) {
                var ob = new Object();

                ob.ModelID = temp[i].ModelID;
                if (temp[i].ModelID == CarModelID) {
                    ob.Hits = temp[i].Hits + 1;
                }
                else {
                    ob.Hits = temp[i].Hits;
                }
                ob.LastScore = Score;
                if (temp[i].Hits + InitialValue == 2) {
                    if (temp[i].ModelID == CarModelID) {
                        ob.Score = Score + temp[i].Score + temp[i].LastScore;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRB(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                        flag = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        ob.Score = temp[i].Score;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRB(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                    }
                }
                else if (temp[i].Hits + InitialValue > 2) {
                    if (temp[i].ModelID == CarModelID) {

                        ob.Score = Score + temp[i].Score;
                        //alert("in model 2:: " + ob.Score + "   " + temp[i].Score + "   " + Score);
                        flag = true;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRB(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        ob.Score = temp[i].Score;
                        if (ob.Score >= HighestValue) {
                            HighestValue = ob.Score;
                            HighestvalueModel = ob.ModelID;
                            SETMOICookieRB(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
                        }
                    }
                }
                //alert("in model else:: " + ob.ModelID + "   " + ob.LastScore + "   " + ob.Score + "   " + ob.Hits);
                arr.push(ob);
            }
        }

        if (flag == false) {
            obj.ModelID = CarModelID;
            obj.Hits = InitialValue;
            obj.LastScore = Score;
            obj.Score = 0;
            if (obj.Score >= HighestValue) {
                HighestvalueModel = obj.ModelID;
                SETMOICookieRB(HighestvalueModel, domainValue);
            }
            arr.push(obj);
        }

        var objWarp = new Object();
        objWarp.models = arr;
        var val = JSON.stringify(objWarp);
        //alert("val:: "+val);
        //set cookie date expired
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();

        //create cookie
        document.cookie = cookie_key + "=" + val + ";domain=." + domainValue + ";path=/";

    }

    function SETMOICookieRB(HighestvalueModel, domainValue) {
        //alert("Moi Cookie");
        var arr = new Array();
        var obj = new Object();
        obj.ModelID = HighestvalueModel;
        arr.push(obj);
        var objWarp = new Object();
        objWarp.models = arr;
        var val = JSON.stringify(objWarp);
        //alert("Value ::"+val);
        //set cookie date expired
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
        //create cookie
        document.cookie = "MOI_Temp" + "=" + val + expires + ";domain=." + domainValue + ";path=/";
        //alert(getCookie("MOI")[0].ModelID);
    }

    function includeRoad65Js(jsFilePath) {
        var js = document.createElement("script");
        js.type = "text/javascript";
        js.src = jsFilePath;

        document.body.appendChild(js);

    }

    //For PT only jira -1494
    function firePTpixelCodeRTB(modelName) {
        try {

            console.log('firePTpixelCode RTB | for modelName:' + modelName);
            if (modelName == null || modelName == "")
                return;
            modelName = modelName.toLowerCase();

            if (modelName.indexOf("asx") > -1) {

                console.log('firePTpixelCode | for asx:');

                fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                    content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                    content_category: 'ASX'
                });
            }
            else
                if (modelName.indexOf("space star") > -1) {

                    console.log('firePTpixelCode | for space star');

                    fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                        content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                        content_category: 'SpaceStar'
                    });
                }
                else
                    if (modelName.indexOf("outlander di") > -1) {

                        console.log('firePTpixelCode | for outlander di');

                        fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                            content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                            content_category: 'Outlander-Did'
                        });
                    }
                    else
                        if (modelName.indexOf("outlander") > -1 && modelName.indexOf("phev") > -1) {

                            console.log('firePTpixelCode | for outlander phev');

                            fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                                content_category: 'Outlander-Phev'
                            });
                        }
                        else
                            if (modelName.indexOf("i-miev") > -1) {

                                console.log('firePTpixelCode | for i-miev');

                                fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                    content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                                    content_category: 'iMiEV'
                                });
                            }
                            else
                                if (modelName.indexOf("l200") > -1) {

                                    console.log('firePTpixelCode | for l200');

                                    fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                        content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                                        content_category: 'L200'
                                    });
                                }
                                else
                                    if (modelName.indexOf("pajero") > -1) {

                                        console.log('firePTpixelCode | for pajero');

                                        fbq('track', 'CompleteRegistration', {
                                            content_name: 'PedirCatalogo',
                                            content_category: 'Pajero'
                                        });
                                    }
                                    else {
                                        console.log('No! pixel code has been fire in PedirCatalogo firePTpixelCode | for modelName:' + modelName);
                                    }

        }
        catch (e) {
            console.log('Error! occour in RTB firePTpixelCode | for modelName:' + modelName);
            console.error(e);
        }
    }

    }

    function FillPromoScriptRB(objPromo) {

        if (objPromo != null) {
            var ifrm = document.getElementById('RTBPromoFrame');
            ifrm = (ifrm.contentWindow) ? ifrm.contentWindow : (ifrm.contentDocument.document) ? ifrm.contentDocument.document : ifrm.contentDocument;
            ifrm.document.open();
            ifrm.document.write(objPromo);
            ifrm.document.close();
        }

    }

    function ExecutePromotionalScriptRTB(hasVal) {

        if (hasVal) {
            FillPromoScriptRB(objPromoScriptRTB)
        }
        else {
            var actualUrl = window.location.pathname;
            var HashUrl = window.location.hash;
            var hostUrl = document.location.protocol + "//" + document.location.hostname;
            var pageUrl;
            if (HashUrl != "") {
                pageUrl = actualUrl + HashUrl;
            }
            else { pageUrl = actualUrl; }
            promourl = pageUrl;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "json",
                data: { 'CallingUrl': pageUrl },
                url: hostUrl + "/layouts/Handlers/GetPromotionalScriptDetails.ashx",
                success: function (data, status) {
                    objPromoScriptRTB = data;
                    FillPromoScriptRB(data);
                },
                error: function (request, status, error) {
                    //alert(status);
                }
            });
        }



    }

    //Function for disable 2nd car model on selection of the 1st car model
    function hide2ndCarmodel() {

        var dropCarModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1");
        var dropCarModel2 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel2");
        if (dropCarModel1.length == 0 || dropCarModel2.length == 0) {
            return;
        }

        $(dropCarModel1).change(function () {
            var parentvalue = $(dropCarModel1).find("option:selected").text();
            $(dropCarModel2).each(function () {
                $(dropCarModel2).find("option").removeAttr("disabled");
            });
            var select2ndCarText = $(dropCarModel2).find("option")[0].text;
            $(dropCarModel2).find("option[value='" + parentvalue + "']").attr("disabled", "disabled");
            $(dropCarModel2).next("span").children().text(select2ndCarText);

        });
    }

    //Function for disable 2nd car model on Model Page load
    function hide2ndCarmodelonLoad() {
        var dropCarModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1");
        var dropCarModel2 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel2");
        if (dropCarModel1.length == 0 || dropCarModel2.length == 0) {
            return;
        }
        //var parentvalue = $('[id$="hdnModelMarketingName"]').val();
        var parentvalue = dropCarModel1.next().children().text();

        $(dropCarModel2).each(function () {
            $(dropCarModel2).find("option").removeAttr("disabled");
        });
        var select2ndCarText = $(dropCarModel2).find("option")[0].text;
        $(dropCarModel2).find("option[value='" + parentvalue + "']").attr("disabled", "disabled");
        $(dropCarModel2).next("span").children().text(select2ndCarText);
		
		//MMEINMTN-1895
		$("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1").removeAttr("disabled")
    }

    function GoogleTrackingModelSelection() {
        if ($("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1").length > 0) {
            //var dropCarModel1 = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1");
            var selectedModel = $("#FrmRequestToBrochure").find("#CarModel1").siblings(".customSelect").children(0).text();//$(dropCarModel1).find("option:selected").text();

            //------------Google Tracking------------------        
            GTMPush('formValidated', 'true');
            GAPush('form', 'model selection brochure request', selectedModel);
            //GAPush('form', 'Event Action', 'Brochure');
            //----------------------------------------------
        }
    }
    function getInternetExplorerVersion() {
        var rv = -1;
        if (navigator.appName == 'Microsoft Internet Explorer') {
            var ua = navigator.userAgent;
            var re = new RegExp("MSIE ([0-9]{1,}[\.0-9]{0,})");
            if (re.exec(ua) != null)
                rv = parseFloat(RegExp.$1);
        }
        else if (navigator.appName == 'Netscape') {
            var ua = navigator.userAgent;
            var re = new RegExp("Trident/.*rv:([0-9]{1,}[\.0-9]{0,})");
            if (re.exec(ua) != null)
                rv = parseFloat(RegExp.$1);
        }
        return rv;
    }

        function changeDivRtdIndexId(obj) {
            var oldid = $(obj).attr('data-prev-href');
            var n = $(obj).attr('href').substring(1);
            n = n.replace(" ", "-");
            //var oldid = $("#"+divId).attr('id');
            //alert(n);
            $("#" + oldid).attr('id', n);
            $(obj).attr('data-prev-href', n);
            window.location.hash = $(obj).attr('data-original-href');

            //------------Google Tracking------------------
            var eventLabel = "";
            if ($(obj).attr('id') == "RequestTestDrive") {
                eventLabel = "request testdrive";
            }
            else {
                eventLabel = "request brochure";
            }
            //alert($(obj).attr('id'));

            GAPush('slider homepage', 'click', eventLabel);
            //----------------------------------------------
        }

        function load360() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-4");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-2");
                ChnageFlipHeight();
            }, 3000);
            setTimeout(function () {
                ChnageFlipHeight();
            }, 2000);
            setTimeout(function () {
                ChnageFlipHeight();
            }, 5000);
        }

        function ChnageFlipHeight() {
            if ($(window).width() < 768) return;

            var flipBackHeight = 0;
            $(".flip-back").each(function (index, element) {
                //console.log($(this).height());
                var img = $($(this).parents(".quickFlip")[0]).find("img")[0];
                if ($(img).height() > 0) {
                    flipBackHeight = $(img).height();
                }
                //console.log($(img).height());
            });
            $(".social-links").each(function (index, element) {
                //alert($(this).height());
                var img = $($(this).parents(".quickFlip")[0]).find("img")[0];
                if ($(img).height() > 0) {
                    flipBackHeight = $(img).height();
                }
            });


            if (flipBackHeight > 0) {
                $(".flip-back").height(flipBackHeight);
                $(".social-links").height(flipBackHeight);
            }


        }


        $(window).load(function () {
           
            //$("#RequestTestDrive").attr('data-prev-href', n);
            //window.location.hash = $("#RequestTestDrive").attr('data-original-href');
            setTimeout(function () {
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-4");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-2");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-5");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-3");
            }, 1000);
            setTimeout(function () {
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-4");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-2");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-5");
                MaintainEqlHeight("#section-3");
            }, 3000);
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            var width = $("#carousel-services-Banner").width();
            if (width > 1600) {
                $("#carousel-services-Banner").addClass('upper');
            }
            else {
                $("#carousel-services-Banner").removeClass('upper')
            }
            MaintainEqlHeight("#section-4");
            MaintainEqlHeight("#section-2");
            MaintainEqlHeight("#section-5");
            MaintainEqlHeight("#section-3");

            if ($.browser.msie && (parseInt($.browser.version, 10) == 8 || parseInt($.browser.version, 10) == 9)) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    ChnageFlipHeight();
                }, 500);
                //quickFlip.flip(2,0,1);
            }

            load360();
        }).resize();   // Run resize on window load


        function MaintainEqlHeight(ParentContainerID) {
            if ($(window).width() < 768) {
                return;
            }
            $(ParentContainerID + " .eql-height").removeAttr("style");
            if ($(ParentContainerID + " .eql-height").length > 0) {
                var maxHeight = 0;
                $(ParentContainerID + " .eql-height").each(function () {
                    if ($(this).height() > maxHeight) {
                        maxHeight = $(this).height();
                    }
                });
                if (maxHeight > 0) {
                    $(ParentContainerID + " .eql-height").height(maxHeight);
                }

            }
        }

            $(".cta-sub-container").css("right", "-60px");
            $(".sticky-call-out").css("right", "-300px");
        });

          <script>
           var isFormSubmitted = false; 
    $(document).ready(function () {
        //$(".btm-link.phone").remove();
        if ($(window).scrollTop() == 0) {
            $("#fixed").hide();
        }
        // Animate the scroll to top
        $('#fixed').click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 300);
        });

        $(".btm-link.phone")
    });


    //var lastScrollTop = 0;
    //$(window).scroll(function (event) {
    //    var st = $(this).scrollTop();
    //    if (st > lastScrollTop) {
    //        console.log("down scroll");
    //    } else {
    //        console.log("up scroll");
    //    }
    //    lastScrollTop = st;
    //});

    $(window).scroll(function (event) {
        if ($(window).scrollTop() == 0) {
            $("#fixed").fadeOut(400);
            return;
        }
        $("#fixed").fadeIn(400);
        var d = $(document).height();
        var w = $(window).height();
        var s = $(this).scrollTop();


        var bottomBound = (parseInt($(".footer").height(), 10) + 47);//* 0.8;
        if ($(".model-secondary-menu--stick").length > 0) {
            bottomBound = bottomBound - parseInt($(".model-secondary-menu--stick").height(), 10) * 0.25
        }
        bottomBound = ($('.sanoma-optin-bar').css("display") == "none" ? 30 : 40);
        if (d - (w + s) < bottomBound) {
            $('#fixed').css({
                bottom: bottomBound// bottomBound - (d - (w + s))
            });
        } else {

            $('#fixed').css({
                bottom: ($('.sanoma-optin-bar').css("display") == "none" ? 30 : 40)
                //bottom: 40
            });
        }
        try
        {
            if (isFormSubmitted) {
                var calculatedheight = parseInt($(".footer").height(), 10) + 47
                $("#fixed").css("bottom", calculatedheight);
                isFormSubmitted = false;
            }
        } catch (e) { console.log(e);}
    });
	
	$(window).load(function(){
		if($.cookie('acceptance') == null)
		{
			setTimeout(function(){ fnVoidAllCookies(); fnCheckForAcceptance(); }, 1000);
			var cpnavurl = $("#hdnCPRM_NavURL").val();
			var domaincurrenturl = top.location.href;
			//console.log("cpnavurl > " + cpnavurl + " | domaincurrenturl > " + domaincurrenturl + " | urlindex > " + domaincurrenturl.indexOf(cpnavurl));
			if(domaincurrenturl.indexOf(cpnavurl) == -1 || $.trim(cpnavurl) == "")
			{
				//$("#cookie-details-overlay").hide();
				$("#cookie-overlay").show();
				var body = document.querySelector('body');
				body.classList.add("no-scroll");
				$("html").css("overflow-x","hidden");
				$("body").css("overflow-x","hidden");
				$("body").css("position","fixed");
				$("html").css("position","fixed");
				
				$(".mobile-menu").hide();
				$(".showMenuLeft").hide();
				$(".mobile-fot-link").remove();
				$("div[id$='_phoneCTAholder']").hide();
			}
		    else
			{
				$(".cta-icons").hide();
				$(".cta-label").hide();
				$(".cta-sub-container").hide();
				$(".footer-link > .main-full").hide();
				$("#top-nav").hide();
				$(".model-menu").hide();
				$(".search").hide();
				$(".mobile-menu").hide();
				$(".showMenuLeft").hide();
				$(".mobile-fot-link").remove();
				$("div[id$='_phoneCTAholder']").hide();
			}
			
		}
		else
		{
			var acceptancedata = $.cookie('acceptance');
			if(acceptancedata == "denied")
			{
				setTimeout(function(){ fnVoidAllCookies(); fnCheckForAcceptance(); }, 1000);
			}
		}
	});
	
	function fnViewDetailPolicy(){
		$("#cookie-overlay").hide();
		//$("#cookie-details-overlay").show();
		var body = document.querySelector('body');
		body.classList.add("no-scroll");
	}
	
	function fnViewPolicy(){
		$("#cookie-overlay").show();
		//$("#cookie-details-overlay").hide();
		var body = document.querySelector('body');
		body.classList.add("no-scroll");
	}
	
	function fnAcceptance()
	{
		$("#cookie-overlay").hide();
		//$("#cookie-details-overlay").hide();
		var body = document.querySelector('body');
		body.classList.remove("no-scroll");
		
		var hostname = $('<a>').prop('href', location.href).prop('hostname');
		$.cookie('acceptance',"accepted",{domain: hostname, expires: 365});
		clearInterval(intervalobj);
		location.reload(true);
	}
	
	function fnDenyCookiePolicy()
	{
		var hostname = $('<a>').prop('href', location.href).prop('hostname');
		$.cookie('acceptance',"denied",{domain: hostname});
		
		location.reload(true);
	}
	
	function fnVoidAllCookies()
	{		
		$.ajax({url: "/Services/CookiesManager.ashx", success: function(result){
			//console.log(result);
		}});
		
	}
	
	var intervalobj = null;
	function fnCheckForAcceptance()
	{
			intervalobj = setInterval(function(){
			if($.cookie('acceptance') == null)
			{
				fnVoidAllCookies();
			}
		}, 1000);
	}

            //For linking of shadowbox
            function changeDivRtdId(obj) {

                var index = $(obj).attr('href');
                var oldid = $(obj).attr('data-prev-href');
                var n = $(obj).attr('href').substring(1);
                n = n.replace(" ", "-");
                $("#" + oldid).attr('id', n);
                $(obj).attr('data-prev-href', n);
               

                //------------Google Tracking------------------
                var eventLabel = "";
                if ($(obj).attr('id') == "RequestTestDrive") {
                    eventLabel = "request testdrive";
                }
                else {
                    eventLabel = "request brochure";
                }
                
                GAPush('expandible', 'click', eventLabel);
                //----------------------------------------------
                window.location.hash = $(obj).attr('data-original-href');
               
            }
            $(function () {
                //alert("Zoeken");
                $("#txtSearchPageMob").addClass("lightText")
                // set default value
                .val("Zoeken")
            // onfocus action
            .focus(function () {
                if ($(this).val() == "Zoeken") {
                    $(this).removeClass("lightText").val("");
                }
                // focus lost action
            }).blur(function () {
                if ($(this).val() == "") {
                    $(this).val("Zoeken").addClass("lightText");
                }
            });
            });

        $(window).load(function () {          
            /*--------For Call 2 Action HashBang Href change ------*/
            $('.call2-action-sticky').find('a').each(function () {
                var popupHref = $(this).attr('data-popup-href');
                if (popupHref != "") {
                    $(this).attr('href', '#' + popupHref);
                }
            });
            $('.call2-action-banner').find('a').each(function () {
                var popupHref = $(this).attr('data-popup-href');
                if (popupHref != "") {
                    $(this).attr('href', '#' + popupHref);
                }
            });
            /*------------------------------------*/
            /*--------For Mobile Slider Menu------*/
            var menuIndex = 0;
            $(".slide-text li").each(function () {
                this.id = this.id + menuIndex;
                menuIndex++;
            });
            /*------------------------------------*/

            resizeMenu();
        });


        $(window).resize(function () {
            resizeMenu();
        });

        function resizeMenu() {
            var liCount = 1;
            $.each($('ul.clearfix').children('li'), function () {
                var liWidth = 155;
                var liMarginLeft = -75;
                var target = $(this);
                var targetUL = $(target).find('ul.sub-menu');

                liCount = $(targetUL).children().length;
                liWidth = parseInt(liWidth * liCount);
                liMarginLeft = parseInt(liMarginLeft * liCount);

                if (document.body.clientWidth > 767) {
                    if ($(target).hasClass("mmemodel") && !$(target).hasClass("active")) {
                        $(target).addClass("active");
                    }
                    $(targetUL).attr("style", "width:" + liWidth + "px;margin-left:" + liMarginLeft + "px");
                }
                else {
                    $(targetUL).removeAttr("style");
                    $(target).removeClass("active");
                }
            });
        }
            try {
                var mmeMainMasterLen = $(".MMEMainMaster").find(".terms-hld").length;
                if (mmeMainMasterLen == 0) {
                    $(".mme-contentblock").each(function () {
                        if ($(".mme-contentblock").parents("#dvFAQContent").length <= 0) {
                            $(".mme-contentblock").parents("li").addClass(" terms-hld clearfix col-full");
                            $(".mme-contentblock").parents("ul").addClass("clearfix");
                        }
                    });

                    $(document).ajaxComplete(function () {
                        $(".mme-contentblock").each(function () {
                            if ($(".mme-contentblock").parents("#dvFAQContent").length <= 0) {
                                $(".mme-contentblock").parents("li").addClass(" terms-hld clearfix col-full");
                                $(".mme-contentblock").parents("ul").addClass("clearfix");
                            }
                        });

                    });
                }
                $(".flexWidget").each(function () {
                    var lenContentblock = 0;
                    lenContentblock = $(this).find(".mme-contentblock").length;
                    if (lenContentblock > 1) {
                        var count = 0;
                        $(this).find(".mme-contentblock").each(function () {
                            if (count > 0) {
                                $(this).parents("li").addClass("multicontentblock");
                            }
                            count = count + 1;
                        });
                    }
                });
            } catch (e) { }

            //For widget flexibility centralization
            $(".columnwidgetlist").each(function () {
                try {
                   
                    //Checking if the item is under target content widget
                    if ($(this).parents(".columnwidgetlist").length > 0) {
                        return;
                    }

                    var licount = $(this).children("li.PBItem").length;
                    var totalColvalue = 0;
                    if (licount > 0) {
                        // if have a atleast one col-full in dropzone
                        if ($(this).children("li.col-full") > 0) {
                            totalColvalue = parseInt(totalColvalue) + 12;
                        }
                        else {                            
                            var widgetCount = 0;
                            $(this).children("li.PBItem").each(function () {
                                widgetCount = parseInt(widgetCount) + 1;
                                if (parseInt(totalColvalue) <= 12) {
                                    if ($(this).is("[class*='col-']")) {
                                        var className = $(this).attr('class');
                                        var colvalue = className.substring(className.indexOf("col-") + 4, className.indexOf("col-") + 6);
                                        totalColvalue = parseInt(totalColvalue) + parseInt($.trim(colvalue));
                                    }                                 
                                }
                            });
                            if (parseInt(widgetCount) > 0 && parseInt(totalColvalue) < 11) {                               
                                if (parseInt(widgetCount) == 1) {
                                    $(this).children("li.PBItem").each(function () {
                                        if ($(this).is("[class*='col-']")) {
                                            $(this).addClass("MMESingleWidgetFlexibilty");
                                            if (!$(this).parents("section").hasClass("MMESingleWidgetFlexibiltySection")) {
                                                if ($(this).parents("section").hasClass("fluid-width pos-rel")) {
                                                    $(this).parents("section").addClass("MMESingleWidgetFlexibiltySection");
                                                }

                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                                else {
                                    $(this).children("li.PBItem").each(function () {
                                        if ($(this).is("[class*='col-']")) {
                                            $(this).addClass("MMEMultipleWidgetFlexibilty");
                                            if (!$(this).parents("section").hasClass("MMEMultipleWidgetFlexibiltySection")) {
                                                if ($(this).parents("section").hasClass("fluid-width pos-rel")) {
                                                    $(this).parents("section").addClass("MMEMultipleWidgetFlexibiltySection");
                                                }
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                }

                                // 604
                                if (widgetCount > 0)
                                {
                                    var colAllignment="";
                                    var colDataFound = "false";
                                    $(this).children("li.PBItem").each(function () {
                                        if ($(this).is("[class*='-wa']") && colDataFound == "false") {                                           
                                            if($(this).hasClass("left-wa"))
                                            {
                                                colAllignment = "left-wa";
                                                colDataFound = "true";
                                            } else if ($(this).hasClass("right-wa"))
                                            {
                                                colAllignment = "right-wa";
                                                colDataFound = "true";
                                            }
                                            else if ($(this).hasClass("center-wa"))
                                            {
                                                colAllignment = "center-wa";
                                                colDataFound = "true";
                                            }
                                        }

                                    });

                                
                                    if (colAllignment == "center-wa" || colAllignment == "") {
                                        setTimeout(function () {

                                            $(this).parents("section").addClass("section-wa section-center-wa");
                                        }, 500);
                                       

                                    } else { $(this).parents("section").addClass("section-wa"); }
                                }
                               
                                if (colAllignment == "center-wa") {
                                    $(this).children("li.PBItem:first").css('margin', '0');
                                }
                                // 604
                                var className = $(this).find('aside:first').attr('class');
                                if (className.indexOf('col-') > -1) {
                                    $(this).find("aside:first").css('margin', '0');
                                }
                                 
                            }
                        }
                    }
                } catch(e) { }
            });

            
        //]]>
    </script>

         document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

                     var script = document.createElement("script");
                     script.setAttribute("async", true);
                     var data = JSON.stringify(config);
                     script.src = "//js.buto.tv/" + type + "/" + data;
                     var s = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
                     s.parentNode.insertBefore(script, s);
                 };

                 var videos = document.querySelectorAll('.buto_video');

                 for (i = 0; i < videos.length; i++) {
                     el = videos[i];
                     id = el.id.replace('buto_', '');
                     config = { object_id: id }
                     if (el.getAttribute('data-width')) {
                         config.width = el.getAttribute('data-width');

                         config.height = el.getAttribute('data-height');
                     }
                     loadPlayer('video', config);
                 }

                     loadPlayer('playlist', config);
                 }

             }

    $(window).resize(function () {

    });
    var toplogo_pos = $(".logo-link").width() + $(".logo-link").position().left;
    console.log("Top Logo Area on Load: " + toplogo_pos);
    var reset_topafter = $("#top-nav .nav > li:first").position().left;
    reset_topafter = reset_topafter + 25;
    toplogo_pos = toplogo_pos + 75;
    var reset_after = toplogo_pos + 150;
    var base_topmenu_fsize = "10";
    var base_modelmenu_fsize = "9";

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        try {
            if ($(".model-menu ul.clearfix > li").length >= 10) {
                $(".model-menu ul.clearfix > li > a").css({ "font-size": "9px" });
            }
            $("#top-nav").css({ "top": "0px" });
        } catch (e)
        { }
    });

    function setNavigationFont() {
        //$("#spDisplayPos").html(document.body.clientWidth);
        var client_width = document.body.clientWidth;
        var logo_pos = $(".logo-link").width() + $(".logo-link").position().left;
        console.log("Top Logo Area: " + logo_pos);
        //var logo_pos_top = logo_pos - 50;
        var logo_pos_top = logo_pos + 10;
        logo_pos = logo_pos + 50;
        var posLeft_modelmenu = $(".model-menu ul.clearfix > li:first").position().left;
        var posLeft_topmenu = $("#top-nav").position().left;

        /*
		$(".model-menu ul.clearfix > li:first > span").remove();
		$("<span>" + parseInt(reset_topafter) + " | " + parseInt(posLeft_topmenu) + "</span>").insertBefore(".model-menu ul.clearfix > li:first > a");
		console.log("***********************************************");
        console.log("logo_pos_top For Top Menu: " + logo_pos_top);
        console.log("logo_pos For Model Menu: " + logo_pos);
        console.log("Model Menu Left: " + posLeft_modelmenu);
        console.log("Top Menu Left: " + $("#top-nav").position().left);
        console.log("***********************************************");
        */

        if (logo_pos > posLeft_modelmenu) {
            $(".model-menu ul.clearfix > li > a").css({ "font-size": base_modelmenu_fsize + "px" });
            base_modelmenu_fsize = (base_modelmenu_fsize == "9" ? base_modelmenu_fsize : (parseInt(base_modelmenu_fsize) - 3).toString());
        }
        else if (posLeft_modelmenu > reset_after) {
            base_modelmenu_fsize = (base_modelmenu_fsize == "15" ? base_modelmenu_fsize : (parseInt(base_modelmenu_fsize) + 3).toString());
            $(".model-menu ul.clearfix li>a").css({ "font-size": base_modelmenu_fsize + "px" });
        }

        if (logo_pos_top > posLeft_topmenu) {
            $("#top-nav .nav li a").css({ "font-size": base_topmenu_fsize + "px" });
            base_topmenu_fsize = (base_topmenu_fsize == "10" ? base_topmenu_fsize : (parseInt(base_topmenu_fsize) - 2).toString());
            $("#top-nav").css({ "top": "0px" });
        }
        else if (posLeft_topmenu > reset_topafter) {
            base_topmenu_fsize = (base_topmenu_fsize == "14" ? base_topmenu_fsize : (parseInt(base_topmenu_fsize) + 2).toString());
            $("#top-nav .nav li a").css({ "font-size": base_topmenu_fsize + "px" });
            $("#top-nav").css({ "top": "0px" });
        }

    }
    </script>
